@ITA_MAX_INFANTRY_TEMPLATES = 4
@ITA_MAX_ANTI_TANK_TEMPLATES = 4
@MAX_MOTORIZED_TEMPLATES = 4
@ITA_MAX_MED_ARMOR_TEMPLATES = 4
@ITA_MAX_HV_ARMOR_TEMPLATES = 4

EAI_division_design_strategies = {
	
	
	if = { limit = { EAI_nation_specific_infantry = yes }
		
		meta_effect = {
			text = {
				EAI_infantry_templates/[TAG] = yes 
			}
			TAG = "[Root.GetTag]"
		}
		
	}
	else = {
		EAI_infantry_templates = yes 
	}
	
	if = { limit = { EAI_nation_specific_alternative_infantry = yes } #2nd Infantry role for special purposes
		
		meta_effect = {
			text = {
				EAI_alternative_infantry_templates/[TAG] = yes 
			}
			TAG = "[Root.GetTag]"
		}
		
	}
	
	if = { limit = { EAI_nation_specific_light_infantry = yes }
		
		meta_effect = {
			text = {
				EAI_light_infantry_templates/[TAG] = yes 
			}
			TAG = "[Root.GetTag]"
		}
		
	}
	
	if = { limit = { EAI_nation_specific_marines = yes }
		
		meta_effect = {
			text = {
				EAI_marines_templates/[TAG] = yes 
			}
			TAG = "[Root.GetTag]"
		}
		
	}
	
	if = { limit = { EAI_nation_specific_mountaineers = yes }
		
		meta_effect = {
			text = {
				EAI_mountaineer_templates/[TAG] = yes 
			}
			TAG = "[Root.GetTag]"
		}
		
	}
	
	if = { limit = { EAI_nation_specific_motorized = yes }
		
		meta_effect = {
			text = {
				EAI_motorized_templates/[TAG] = yes 
			}
			TAG = "[Root.GetTag]"
		}
		
	}
	
	if = { limit = { EAI_nation_specific_cavalry = yes }
		
		meta_effect = {
			text = {
				EAI_cavalry_templates/[TAG] = yes 
			}
			TAG = "[Root.GetTag]"
		}
		
	}
	else_if = { limit = { NOT = { has_country_flag = { flag = EAI_motorized_template value = @MAX_MOTORIZED_TEMPLATES } } }

		#EAI_motorized_templates = yes 
		
	}
	
	if = { limit = { EAI_nation_specific_medium_armor = yes }
			
		meta_effect = {
			text = {
				EAI_medium_armor_templates/[TAG] = yes 
			}
			TAG = "[Root.GetTag]"
		}
		
	}	
	
	if = { limit = { EAI_nation_specific_heavy_armor = yes }
			
		meta_effect = {
			text = {
				EAI_nation_specific_heavy_armor/[TAG] = yes 
			}
			TAG = "[Root.GetTag]"
		}
		
	}	
	
	if = { limit = { NOT = { has_country_flag = EAI_suppression_template } }
			
		EAI_generic_suppression = yes 
		
	}	
	
	update_all_subunits = yes
}
EAI_generic_suppression = {
	set_country_flag = { flag = EAI_suppression_template value = 1 }
	division_template = {
		name = "Suppression Division"			
		template_counter = 209
			
		regiments = {
			cavalry = { x = 0 y = 0 }
			cavalry = { x = 0 y = 1 }
			
			cavalry = { x = 1 y = 0 }
			cavalry = { x = 1 y = 1 }
		}
		support = {
			military_police = { x = 0 y = 0 } 
		}

		priority = 0
	}
}

EAI_infantry_templates = {	
	if = {
		limit = {
			NOT = { has_country_flag = EAI_infantry_template }
			
			#CONDITIONS
			always = no
			
		}
		set_country_flag = { flag = EAI_infantry_template value = 1 }
		division_template = {
			name = "Infantry Division"			
			template_counter = 114
			
			regiments = {
				infantry = { x = 0 y = 0 }
				infantry = { x = 0 y = 1 }
				infantry = { x = 0 y = 2 }
				
				infantry = { x = 1 y = 0 }
				infantry = { x = 1 y = 1 }
				infantry = { x = 1 y = 2 }
				
				infantry = { x = 2 y = 0 }
				infantry = { x = 2 y = 1 }
				infantry = { x = 2 y = 2 }
				infantry = { x = 2 y = 3 }
		
				artillery_brigade = { x = 3 y = 0 }		
				artillery_brigade = { x = 3 y = 1 }		
				artillery_brigade = { x = 3 y = 2 }		
				anti_tank_brigade = { x = 3 y = 3 }
			}
			support = {
				DIV_HQ = { x = 0 y = 0 } 	
				engineer = { x = 0 y = 1 }
				recon = { x = 0 y = 2 }
				combat_engineer = { x = 0 y = 3 }
				logistics_company = { x = 0 y = 4 }
				
				field_hospital = { x = 1 y = 0 } 
			}

			priority = 1
		}
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				EAI_anti_air_design_focus = yes 
			}
			set_country_flag = EAI_use_anti_air_support
			
			division_template = {
				name = "Infantry Division"			
				template_counter = 114
			
				regiments = {

					infantry = { x = 2 y = 2 }
					infantry = { x = 2 y = 3 }
			
					artillery_brigade = { x = 3 y = 0 }		
					artillery_brigade = { x = 3 y = 1 }		
					artillery_brigade = { x = 3 y = 2 }		
					anti_tank_brigade = { x = 3 y = 3 }
				}
				support = {
					DIV_HQ = { x = 0 y = 0 } 	
					engineer = { x = 0 y = 1 }
					recon = { x = 0 y = 2 }
					combat_engineer = { x = 0 y = 3 }
					logistics_company = { x = 0 y = 4 }
					
					field_hospital = { x = 1 y = 0 } 
					anti_air_heavy = { x = 1 y = 1 } 
				}

				priority = 1
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				EAI_anti_tank_design_focus = yes 
			}
			set_country_flag = EAI_use_anti_tank_support
			
			division_template = {
				name = "Infantry Division"			
				template_counter = 114
			
				regiments = {
					infantry = { x = 0 y = 0 }
					infantry = { x = 0 y = 1 }
					infantry = { x = 0 y = 2 }
					
					infantry = { x = 1 y = 0 }
					infantry = { x = 1 y = 1 }
					infantry = { x = 1 y = 2 }
					
					infantry = { x = 2 y = 0 }
					infantry = { x = 2 y = 1 }
					infantry = { x = 2 y = 2 }
					infantry = { x = 2 y = 3 }
			
					artillery_brigade = { x = 3 y = 0 }		
					artillery_brigade = { x = 3 y = 1 }		
					artillery_brigade = { x = 3 y = 2 }		
					anti_tank_brigade = { x = 3 y = 3 }
				}
				support = {
					DIV_HQ = { x = 0 y = 0 } 	
					engineer = { x = 0 y = 1 }
					recon = { x = 0 y = 2 }
					combat_engineer = { x = 0 y = 3 }
					logistics_company = { x = 0 y = 4 }
					
					field_hospital = { x = 1 y = 0 } 
					anti_tank_heavy = { x = 1 y = 1 } 
				}

				priority = 1
			}
		}
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				EAI_anti_air_design_focus = yes 
				EAI_anti_tank_design_focus = yes 
			}
			
			division_template = {
				name = "Infantry Division"			
				template_counter = 114
			
				regiments = {
					infantry = { x = 0 y = 0 }
					infantry = { x = 0 y = 1 }
					infantry = { x = 0 y = 2 }

					artillery_brigade = { x = 3 y = 2 }		
					anti_tank_brigade = { x = 3 y = 3 }
				}
				support = {

					engineer = { x = 0 y = 1 }
					recon = { x = 0 y = 2 }
					combat_engineer = { x = 0 y = 3 }

					field_hospital = { x = 1 y = 0 }

				priority = 1

EAI_infantry_templates/FRA = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			NOT = { has_country_flag = EAI_infantry_template }
			
			#CONDITIONS
			OR = {
				AND = {
					ai_has_role_template = alternative_infantry
					NOT = { ai_has_role_division = alternative_infantry }
				}
				date > 1938.1.1
				has_war = yes
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = { flag = EAI_infantry_template value = 1 }
		set_temp_variable = { temp = num_equipment_in_armies@fra_infantry_tank_equipment }
		add_to_temp_variable = { temp = num_equipment@fra_infantry_tank_equipment }
		delete_unit_template_and_units = {
			division_template = "Brigade de Chars de Combat"
		}
		add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
			type = fra_infantry_tank_equipment
			amount = temp
			producer = FRA
		}
		division_template = {
			name = "Infantry Division"			
			template_counter = 114
			
			regiments = {
				infantry = {x = 0 y = 0}
				infantry = {x = 0 y = 1}
				infantry = {x = 0 y = 2}

				infantry = {x = 1 y = 0}
				infantry = {x = 1 y = 1}
				infantry = {x = 1 y = 2}
				
				infantry = {x = 2 y = 0}
				infantry = {x = 2 y = 1}
				infantry = {x = 2 y = 2}
				
				artillery_brigade = { x = 3 y = 0 }
				artillery_brigade = { x = 3 y = 1 }
				artillery_brigade = { x = 3 y = 2 }
				anti_tank_brigade =  { x = 3 y = 3 }
				
				french_infantry_tank =  { x = 4 y = 0 }
			}
			support = {
				DIV_HQ = { x = 0 y = 0 }
				engineer = { x = 0 y = 1 }
				maintenance_company = { x = 0 y = 2 }
				
				field_hospital = { x = 1 y = 0 }
				recon = { x = 1 y = 1 }
				logistics_company = { x = 1 y = 2 }
			}

			priority = 1
		}
	}
}

EAI_infantry_templates/HUN = {

			division_template = {

				}
			}
		}
		else_if = { limit = { has_tech = tech_logistics_company NOT = { has_tech = tech_field_hospital } }
			set_country_flag = { flag = EAI_infantry_template value = 3 }
			division_template = {
				name = "Infantry Division"	
				template_counter = 114

					infantry = { x = 0 y = 0 }
					infantry = { x = 0 y = 1 }
					
					infantry = { x = 1 y = 0 }
					infantry = { x = 1 y = 1 }
					
					infantry = { x = 2 y = 0 }
					infantry = { x = 2 y = 1 }

					artillery_brigade = { x = 3 y = 0 }		
					artillery_brigade = { x = 3 y = 1 }	
					artillery_brigade = { x = 3 y = 2 }	
				}
				support = {
					DIV_HQ = { x = 0 y = 0 }
					recon = { x = 0 y = 1 } 
					engineer = { x = 0 y = 2 }
					logistics_company = { x = 0 y = 3 }
				}
			}
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			OR = {
				has_country_flag = { flag = EAI_infantry_template value = 2 }
				has_country_flag = { flag = EAI_infantry_template value = 3 }
			}

				artillery_brigade = { x = 3 y = 1 }	
				artillery_brigade = { x = 3 y = 2 }

			}

		}

				infantry = { x = 1 y = 2 }
				
				infantry = { x = 2 y = 0 }
				infantry = { x = 2 y = 1 }
				infantry = { x = 2 y = 2 }

				artillery_brigade = { x = 3 y = 0 }

		limit = {
			has_country_flag = { flag = EAI_infantry_template value = 2 }
			
			check_variable = { field_strength > 0.9 }
			has_tech = interwar_antiair
			has_tech = interwar_antitank
		}
		set_country_flag = { flag = EAI_infantry_template value = 3 }
		division_template = {
			name = "Infantry Division"	
			template_counter = 114
			
			regiments = {
				infantry = { x = 0 y = 0 }
				infantry = { x = 0 y = 1 }
				infantry = { x = 0 y = 2 }
				
				infantry = { x = 1 y = 0 }
				infantry = { x = 1 y = 1 }
				infantry = { x = 1 y = 2 }
				
				infantry = { x = 2 y = 0 }
				infantry = { x = 2 y = 1 }
				infantry = { x = 2 y = 2 }

				artillery_brigade = { x = 3 y = 0 }		
				artillery_brigade = { x = 3 y = 1 }		
				artillery_brigade = { x = 3 y = 2 }		
				anti_tank_brigade = { x = 3 y = 3 }	
			}
			support = {
				DIV_HQ = { x = 0 y = 0 }
				recon = { x = 0 y = 1 } 
				engineer = { x = 0 y = 2 }
				anti_air = { x = 0 y = 3 }
				
				logistics_company = { x = 1 y = 0 }
				field_hospital = { x = 1 y = 0 }
				mount_support = { x = 1 y = 0 }
			}
		}
	}
}

		AI_bonus_4

update_all_subunits = {
	hidden_effect = {
		set_technology = { subunit_1 = 0 }
		set_technology = { subunit_1 = 1 }
	}
}

adjust_laws_for_manpower_shortage = {

	if = {
		limit = {
			has_idea = cons_volunteer 
		}
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { has_idea = age_18 }
				can_take_age_18 = yes
			}
			
			add_ideas = age_18
			
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				can_take_cons_one = yes 
			}
			add_ideas = cons_one
		}
		
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			has_idea = cons_one
		}
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { has_idea = age_17 }
				can_take_age_17 = yes
			}
			
			add_ideas = age_17
			
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				can_take_cons_two = yes 
			}
			add_ideas = cons_two
		}
		
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			has_idea = cons_two
		}
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { has_idea = age_17 }
				can_take_age_17 = yes
			}
			
			add_ideas = age_17
			
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				can_take_cons_three = yes 
			}
			add_ideas = cons_three
		}
		
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			has_idea = cons_three
		}
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { has_idea = age_16 }
				can_take_age_16 = yes
			}
			
			add_ideas = age_16
			
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				can_take_cons_expanded_draft = yes 
			}
			add_ideas = cons_expanded_draft
		}
		
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			has_idea = cons_expanded_draft
		}
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { has_idea = age_15 }
				can_take_age_15 = yes
			}
			
			add_ideas = age_15
			
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				can_take_cons_extensive_draft = yes 
			}
			add_ideas = cons_extensive_draft
		}
		
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			has_idea = cons_extensive_draft
		}
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { has_idea = age_14 }
				can_take_age_14 = yes
			}
			
			add_ideas = age_14
			
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				can_take_cons_barrel = yes 
			}
			add_ideas = cons_barrel
		}
		
	}
}

create_infantry_equipment_variant = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_tech = advanced_infantry_weapons
		}
		meta_effect = {
			text = {
				create_equipment_variant = { 
					name = "Infantry Equipment" 
					type = infantry_equipment_3
					#parent_version = [INFANTRY_EQUIPMENT_PARENT]
					upgrades = { 
						weapons_quality_upgrade = [LEVEL_1]
						weapons_rifle_grenade_upgrade = [LEVEL_2]
						weapons_smoke_grenade_upgrade = [LEVEL_3]
					}
				}
			}
			#INFANTRY_EQUIPMENT_PARENT = "1"
			LEVEL_1 = infantry_equipment_lvl_1
			LEVEL_2 = infantry_equipment_lvl_2
			LEVEL_3 = infantry_equipment_lvl_3
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			has_tech = improved_infantry_weapons
		}
		meta_effect = {
			text = {
				create_equipment_variant = { 
					name = "Infantry Equipment" 
					type = infantry_equipment_2
					#parent_version = [INFANTRY_EQUIPMENT_PARENT]
					upgrades = { 
						weapons_quality_upgrade = [LEVEL_1]
						weapons_rifle_grenade_upgrade = [LEVEL_2]
						weapons_smoke_grenade_upgrade = [LEVEL_3]
					}
				}
			}
			#INFANTRY_EQUIPMENT_PARENT = "1"
			LEVEL_1 = infantry_equipment_lvl_1
			LEVEL_2 = infantry_equipment_lvl_2
			LEVEL_3 = infantry_equipment_lvl_3
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			has_tech = infantry_weapons1
		}
		meta_effect = {
			text = {
				create_equipment_variant = { 
					name = "Infantry Equipment" 
					type = infantry_equipment_1
					#parent_version = [INFANTRY_EQUIPMENT_PARENT]
					upgrades = { 
						weapons_quality_upgrade = [LEVEL_1]
						weapons_rifle_grenade_upgrade = [LEVEL_2]
						weapons_smoke_grenade_upgrade = [LEVEL_3]
					}
				}
			}
			#INFANTRY_EQUIPMENT_PARENT = "1"
			LEVEL_1 = infantry_equipment_lvl_1
			LEVEL_2 = infantry_equipment_lvl_2
			LEVEL_3 = infantry_equipment_lvl_3
		}
	}
	
	if = {
		limit = {
			set_temp_variable = { max_upgrades = @INFANTRY_EQUIPMENT_VARIANT_1_MAX }
			add_to_temp_variable = { max_upgrades = @INFANTRY_EQUIPMENT_VARIANT_2_MAX }
			add_to_temp_variable = { max_upgrades = @INFANTRY_EQUIPMENT_VARIANT_3_MAX }
			
			set_temp_variable = { upgrades = infantry_equipment_lvl_1 }
			add_to_temp_variable = { upgrades = infantry_equipment_lvl_2 }
			add_to_temp_variable = { upgrades = infantry_equipment_lvl_3 }
			
			check_variable = { max_upgrades = upgrades } 
		}
		set_country_flag = infantry_eq_end
	}
}

			add_to_temp_variable = { upgrades = infantry_uniform_lvl_3 }

		}
		set_country_flag = uniform_eq_end
	}
}

create_support_equipment_variant = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_tech = tech_support
		}
		meta_effect = {
			text = {
				create_equipment_variant = { 
					name = "Support Equipment" 
					type = support_equipment_1
					#parent_version = [SUPPORT_PARENT]
					upgrades = { 
						support_medicine_upgrade = [LEVEL_1]
						support_tools_upgrade = [LEVEL_2]
					}
				}
			}
			#SUPPORT_PARENT = "1"
			LEVEL_1 = support_lvl_1
			LEVEL_2 = support_lvl_2
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			set_temp_variable = { max_upgrades = @SUPPORT_EQUIPMENT_VARIANT_1_MAX }
			add_to_temp_variable = { max_upgrades = @SUPPORT_EQUIPMENT_VARIANT_2_MAX }
			
			set_temp_variable = { upgrades = support_lvl_1 }
			add_to_temp_variable = { upgrades = support_lvl_2 }
			
			check_variable = { max_upgrades = upgrades } 
		}
		set_country_flag = support_eq_end
	}
}

					}
				}
			}
			#INF_AT_PARENT = "1"
			LEVEL_1 = inf_at_lvl_1
			LEVEL_2 = inf_at_lvl_2
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			has_tech = infantry_at_2
		}
		meta_effect = {
			text = {
				create_equipment_variant = { 
					name = "Infantry Anti Tank" 
					type = handheld_at_equipment_1
					#parent_version = [INF_AT_PARENT]
					upgrades = { 
						infantry_antitank_he_upgrade = [LEVEL_1]
						infantry_antitank_sights_upgrade = [LEVEL_2]
					}
				}
			}
			#INF_AT_PARENT = "1"
			LEVEL_1 = inf_at_lvl_1
			LEVEL_2 = inf_at_lvl_2
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			has_tech = infantry_at
		}
		meta_effect = {
			text = {
				create_equipment_variant = { 
					name = "Infantry Anti Tank" 
					type = handheld_at_equipment_0
					#parent_version = [INF_AT_PARENT]
					upgrades = { 
						infantry_antitank_he_upgrade = [LEVEL_1]
						infantry_antitank_sights_upgrade = [LEVEL_2]
					}
				}
			}
			#INF_AT_PARENT = "1"
			LEVEL_1 = inf_at_lvl_1
			LEVEL_2 = inf_at_lvl_2
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			set_temp_variable = { max_upgrades = @INF_AT_EQUIPMENT_VARIANT_1_MAX }
			add_to_temp_variable = { max_upgrades = @INF_AT_EQUIPMENT_VARIANT_2_MAX }
			
			set_temp_variable = { upgrades = inf_at_lvl_1 }
			add_to_temp_variable = { upgrades = inf_at_lvl_2 }
			
			check_variable = { max_upgrades = upgrades } 
		}
		set_country_flag = inf_at_eq_end
	}
}	
			
set_infantry_width = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			NOT = {
				has_country_flag = infantry_width_increase
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = {
			flag = infantry_width_increase
			days = 90 
			value = 1
		}
	}
}
			
set_infantry_focus = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { enemy_max_armor > max_pierce }
		}
		set_country_flag = INFANTRY_AT_FOCUS
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { enemy_max_armor > max_pierce }
		}
		set_country_flag = INFANTRY_AT_FOCUS
	}
}

set_starting_template_focus = {
	set_country_flag = infantry_MED_ARTY
	
}

set_starting_template_width = {
	set_variable = { infantry_width = 32 }
	
	meta_effect = {
		text = {
			set_country_flag = infantry_[WIDTH]_width
		}
		WIDTH = infantry_width
	}
	
}

set_starting_doctrine = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			sf_doctrine = yes 
		}
		set_country_flag = sf_doctrine
	}
}

set_template_flags = {
	meta_effect = {
		text = {
			set_country_flag = [DOCTRINE]_infantry_[WIDTH]_[VARIANT]/FOCUS:[FOCUS] = yes
		}
		DOCTRINE = "[Root.GetDoctrine]"
		WIDTH = infantry_width
		VARIANT = "[Root.GetInfantryTemplateVariant]"
		FOCUS = "[Root.GetInfantryTemplateFocus]"
	}
}

clear_template_flags = { #always run this before setting new doctrine/width/variant
	meta_effect = {
		text = {
			clr_country_flag = [DOCTRINE]_infantry_[WIDTH]_[VARIANT]
		}
		DOCTRINE = "[Root.GetDoctrine]"
		WIDTH = infantry_width
		VARIANT = "[Root.GetInfantryTemplateVariant]"
	}
}


EAI_replace_ministers_effect = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_political_power > 100 
		}
		
		if = { limit = { original_tag = GER } 
		
			if = { limit = { 
				
					#MINISTER
					has_idea = goering
					
					#CONDITION TO REMOVE
					has_war = no 
					
					#REASON
					#GER goes for albert_kesselring in buildup to get more Air XP 
				}
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = goering
					add_idea = albert_kesselring
				}
			}
			if = { limit = { 
				
					#MINISTER
					has_idea = albert_kesselring
					
					#CONDITION TO REMOVE
					has_war = yes 
					
					#REASON
					#GER switches to goering when at war 
				}
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = albert_kesselring
					add_idea = goering
				}
			}
			if = { limit = { 
				
					#MINISTER
					has_idea = raeder
					
					#CONDITION TO REMOVE
					OR = {
						has_war = yes 
						date < 1939.1.1
					}
					
					#REASON
					#GER switches to donitz when at war 
				}
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = raeder
					add_idea = donitz
				}
			}
			if = { limit = { 
				
					#MINISTER
					has_idea = Alkett
					
					#CONDITION TO REMOVE
					has_completed_focus = GER_nibelungen_works
					
					#REASON
					#GER switches to Nigelungen Factory
				}
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = Alkett
					add_idea = nibelungenwerke
				}
			}
			if = { limit = { 
				
					#MINISTER
					has_idea = konstantin_von_neurath
					
					#CONDITION TO REMOVE
					date > 1938.6.1
					
					#REASON
					#GER switches to rippentrop
				}
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = konstantin_von_neurath
					add_idea = joachim_von_ribbentrop
				}
			}
			if = { limit = { 
				
					#MINISTER
					has_idea = heinrich_himmler
					
					#CONDITION TO REMOVE
					OR = {
						date > 1939.6.1
						has_war = yes 
					}
					
					#REASON
					#less resistance
				}
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = heinrich_himmler
					add_idea = reinhard_heydrich
				}
			}
			if = { limit = { 
				
					#MINISTER
					has_idea = heinrich_himmler
					
					#CONDITION TO REMOVE
					OR = {
						date > 1939.6.1
						has_war = yes 
					}
					
					#REASON
					#less resistance
				}
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = heinrich_himmler
					add_idea = reinhard_heydrich
				}
			}
			if = { limit = { 
				
					#MINISTER
					has_idea = alfried_krupp
					
					#CONDITION TO REMOVE
					date > 1938.1.1
					
					#REASON
					#switch to MIC construction
				}
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = alfried_krupp
					add_idea = walther_funk
				}
			}
			if = { limit = { 
				
					#MINISTER
					has_idea = GER_franz_schlegelberger
					
					#CONDITION TO REMOVE
					has_stability > 0.95
					
					#REASON
					#switch to supply bonus
				}
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = GER_franz_schlegelberger
					add_idea = GER_wilhelm_ohnesorge
				}
			}
			if = { limit = { 
				
					#MINISTER
					has_idea = rudolf_hess
					
					#CONDITION TO REMOVE
					date > 1936.3.1
					
					#REASON
					#switch to consumer bonus
				}
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = rudolf_hess
					add_idea = roland_freisler
				}
			}
			if = { limit = { 
				
					#MINISTER
					has_idea = roland_freisler
					
					#CONDITION TO REMOVE
					date > 1939.1.1
					
					#REASON
					#switch to pp bonus
				}
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = roland_freisler
					add_idea = martin_bormann
				}
			}
		}
		
		if = { limit = { original_tag = ENG } 
		
			if = { limit = { 
				
					#MINISTER
					has_idea = stewart_menzies
					
					#CONDITION TO REMOVE
					date > 1937.1.1
					
					#REASON
					#convoy retreat and detection bonus
				}
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = stewart_menzies
					add_idea = ENG_intelguy
				}
			}
			if = { limit = { 
				
					#MINISTER
					has_idea = neville_chamberlain
					
					#CONDITION TO REMOVE
					date > 1938.4.1
					
					#REASON
					#MIC buildup
				}
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = neville_chamberlain
					add_idea = ENG_maxwell_aitken
				}
			}
			if = { limit = { 
				
					#MINISTER
					has_idea = cyril_deverell
					
					#CONDITION TO REMOVE
					date > 1937.1.1
					
					#REASON
					#retreat speed
				}
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = cyril_deverell
					add_idea = edmund_ironside
				}
			}
			
			if = { limit = { 
				
					#MINISTER
					has_idea = ernle_chatfield
					
					#CONDITION TO REMOVE
					date > 1937.1.1
					
					#REASON
					#MIC buildup
				}
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = ernle_chatfield
					add_idea = dudley_pound
				}
			}
			if = { limit = { 
				
					#MINISTER
					has_idea = dudley_pound
					
					#CONDITION TO REMOVE
					NOT = { has_country_flag = chatfield_retires }
					convoy_threat < 0.05
					
					#REASON
					#switch to fleet bonus
				}
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = dudley_pound
					add_idea = ernle_chatfield
				}
			}
			
		}
				
	}
}

@ST_STABILITY_NEED_MAX = 90 #At 90% Stability ai will do for stability decisions is <0
@ST_STABILITY_NEED_WEIGHT = 0.1
@ST_STABILITY_WEEKLY_NEED_WEIGHT = -250

@ST_STABILITY_GAIN_WEIGHT = 5.0 #weight of stab gained by decision 
@ST_WAR_SUPPORT_GAIN_WEIGHT = 2.5 #weight of warsupport gained by decision 

EAI_stability_score_debug = {
	if = { limit = { is_ai = yes }
	set_temp_variable = { stability_score = @ST_STABILITY_NEED_MAX } #if stability is 100 AI will do for stability decisions is 0 

	set_temp_variable = { stability_temp = has_stability }
	multiply_temp_variable = { stability_temp = 100 }
	
	subtract_from_temp_variable = { stability_score = stability_temp }
	multiply_temp_variable = { stability_score = @ST_STABILITY_NEED_WEIGHT }
	
	custom_effect_tooltip = "||| [?stability_score|3] Stability Need"
	
	if = { limit = { check_variable = { modifier@stability_weekly < 0 } }
	
	set_temp_variable = { stability_weekly_temp = modifier@stability_weekly }
	multiply_temp_variable = { stability_weekly_temp = @ST_STABILITY_WEEKLY_NEED_WEIGHT }
	
	}
	add_to_temp_variable = { stability_score = stability_weekly_temp }
	
	custom_effect_tooltip = "||| [?stability_weekly_temp|3] Weekly Stability Need"
	custom_effect_tooltip = "||| [?stability_score|3] Total Stability Need"
	
	
	#######################################################################################
	### Decision Effect Weighting
	
	divide_temp_variable = { duration = 7 }
	multiply_temp_variable = { stability_weekly = duration }
	multiply_temp_variable = { war_support_weekly = duration }
	
	multiply_temp_variable = { stability_weekly = @ST_STABILITY_GAIN_WEIGHT }
	multiply_temp_variable = { war_support_weekly = @ST_WAR_SUPPORT_GAIN_WEIGHT }
	
	add_to_temp_variable = { stability_weekly = 1 }
	add_to_temp_variable = { war_support_weekly = 1 }
	
	custom_effect_tooltip = "||| x [?stability_weekly|3] Stability Gain"
	custom_effect_tooltip = "||| x [?war_support_weekly|3] War Support Gain"
	
	#######################################################################################
	### Stop Decision Stacking
	
	set_temp_variable = { ai_factor = 1 } #if more than 2% weekly increase AI will stop doing stability decisions entirely
	
	if = { limit = { check_variable = { modifier@stability_weekly > 0 } }
	
	set_temp_variable = { stability_weekly_gain = modifier@stability_weekly }
	multiply_temp_variable = { stability_weekly_gain = 50 }
	
	}
	
	subtract_from_temp_variable = { ai_factor = stability_weekly_gain }
	
	multiply_temp_variable = { stability_score = stability_weekly }
	multiply_temp_variable = { stability_score = war_support_weekly }
	
	
	#######################################################################################
	### Consumer Goods Weighting
	
	if = { 	
		limit = {
			NOT = { check_variable = { consumer_goods = 0 } }
		}
		
		multiply_temp_variable = { consumer_goods = 3 }
		calculate_min_cons_goods_modifier_temp = yes 
		
		set_temp_variable = { cons_goods = modifier@consumer_goods_factor }
		subtract_from_temp_variable = { cons_goods = min_cons_goods_temp }
		add_to_temp_variable = { cons_goods = consumer_goods }
		if = { limit = { check_variable = { cons_goods > 0.15 } }
			multiply_temp_variable = { cons_goods = 50 }
		}
		else_if = { limit = { check_variable = { cons_goods > 0.10 } }
			multiply_temp_variable = { cons_goods = 42.5 }
		}
		else_if = { limit = { check_variable = { cons_goods > 0.05 } }
			multiply_temp_variable = { cons_goods = 33 }
		}
		else_if = { limit = { check_variable = { cons_goods > 0 } }
			multiply_temp_variable = { cons_goods = 25 }
		}
		
		
		subtract_from_temp_variable = { stability_score = cons_goods }
		
		custom_effect_tooltip = "||| -[?cons_goods|3] Consumer Goods"
	}
	
	#######################################################################################
	### Political Power Weighting
	if = { 	
		limit = {
			NOT = { check_variable = { political_power = 0 } }
		}
		
		multiply_temp_variable = { consumer_goods = 3 }
		calculate_min_cons_goods_modifier_temp = yes 
		
		set_temp_variable = { cons_goods = modifier@consumer_goods_factor }
		subtract_from_temp_variable = { cons_goods = min_cons_goods_temp }
		add_to_temp_variable = { cons_goods = consumer_goods }
		if = { limit = { check_variable = { cons_goods > 0.15 } }
			multiply_temp_variable = { cons_goods = 50 }
		}
		else_if = { limit = { check_variable = { cons_goods > 0.10 } }
			multiply_temp_variable = { cons_goods = 42.5 }
		}
		else_if = { limit = { check_variable = { cons_goods > 0.05 } }
			multiply_temp_variable = { cons_goods = 33 }
		}
		else_if = { limit = { check_variable = { cons_goods > 0 } }
			multiply_temp_variable = { cons_goods = 25 }
		}
		
		
		subtract_from_temp_variable = { stability_score = cons_goods }
		
		custom_effect_tooltip = "||| -[?cons_goods|3] Consumer Goods"
	}
		
	multiply_temp_variable = { stability_score = ai_factor }
	custom_effect_tooltip = "||| x[?ai_factor|3] Stacking Prevention"
	
	custom_effect_tooltip = "||| = [?stability_score|3] Final Score"
} }



@WS_WAR_SUPPORT_NEED_MAX = 90 #At 90% War support ai will do for war support decisions is <0
@WS_WAR_SUPPORT_NEED_WEIGHT = 0.05
@WS_WAR_SUPPORT_WEEKLY_NEED_WEIGHT = -150

@WS_WAR_SUPPORT_GAIN_WEIGHT = 3.0 #weight of warsupport gained by decision 
@WS_STABILITY_GAIN_WEIGHT = 1.5 #weight of stab gained by decision 

EAI_war_support_score_debug = {
	if = { limit = { is_ai = yes }
	set_temp_variable = { war_support_score = @WS_WAR_SUPPORT_NEED_MAX } #if war support is 100 AI will do for stability decisions is 0 

	set_temp_variable = { war_support_temp = has_war_support }
	multiply_temp_variable = { war_support_temp = 100 }
	
	subtract_from_temp_variable = { war_support_score = war_support_temp }
	multiply_temp_variable = { war_support_score = @WS_WAR_SUPPORT_NEED_WEIGHT }
	
	custom_effect_tooltip = "||| [?war_support_score|3] War Support Need"
	
	if = { limit = { check_variable = { modifier@war_support_weekly < 0 } }
	
	set_temp_variable = { war_support_weekly_temp = modifier@war_support_weekly }
	multiply_temp_variable = { war_support_weekly_temp = @WS_WAR_SUPPORT_WEEKLY_NEED_WEIGHT }
	
	}
	add_to_temp_variable = { war_support_score = war_support_weekly_temp }
	
	custom_effect_tooltip = "||| [?war_support_weekly_temp|3] Weekly War Support Need"
	custom_effect_tooltip = "||| [?war_support_score|3] Total War Support Need"
	
	
	#######################################################################################
	### Decision Effect Weighting
	
	divide_temp_variable = { duration = 7 }
	multiply_temp_variable = { war_support_weekly = duration }
	multiply_temp_variable = { stability_weekly = duration }
	
	multiply_temp_variable = { war_support_weekly = @WS_WAR_SUPPORT_GAIN_WEIGHT }
	multiply_temp_variable = { stability_weekly = @WS_STABILITY_GAIN_WEIGHT }
	
	add_to_temp_variable = { war_support_weekly = 1 }
	add_to_temp_variable = { stability_weekly = 1 }
	
	custom_effect_tooltip = "||| x [?war_support_weekly|3] War Support Gain"
	custom_effect_tooltip = "||| x [?stability_weekly|3] Stability Gain"
	
	#######################################################################################
	### Stop Decision Stacking
	
	set_temp_variable = { ai_factor = 1 } #if more than 2% weekly increase AI will stop doing war_support decisions entirely
	
	if = { limit = { check_variable = { modifier@war_support_weekly > 0 } }
	
	set_temp_variable = { war_support_weekly_gain = modifier@war_support_weekly }
	multiply_temp_variable = { war_support_weekly_gain = 50 }
	
	}
	
	subtract_from_temp_variable = { ai_factor = war_support_weekly_gain }
	
	multiply_temp_variable = { war_support_score = war_support_weekly }
	multiply_temp_variable = { war_support_score = stability_weekly }
	multiply_temp_variable = { war_support_score = ai_factor }
	
	custom_effect_tooltip = "||| x[?ai_factor|3] Stacking Prevention"
	
	custom_effect_tooltip = "||| = [?war_support_score|3] Final Score"
	
	#######################################################################################
	### Consumer Goods Weighting
} }
